def square(x):
    return x * x

class Counter:
    def __init__(self, start=0):
        self.value = start
    def inc(self):
        self.value += 1
        return self.value

FIM = True

sq = square(2)
ctr = Counter(0)
after = ctr.inc()
total = ctr.value
neg = not flag
both = flag and False

>>>flag

    def inc(self):
        self.value += 1
        return self.value

        self.value = start
    def inc(self):
        self.value += 1
        return self.value

class Counter:
    def __init__(self, start=0):
        self.value = start
    def inc(self):
        self.value += 1
        return self.value

FIM = [1, 2, 3]

sq = square(4)
ctr = Counter(5)
after = ctr.inc()
total = ctr.value
values.append(4)
first = values[0]
